\n\n=== FILENAME: src/app/espace/gestion-reservations/page.tsx ===
"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import {
  Table, TableBody, TableCell, TableHead, TableHeader, TableRow,
} from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/table";
import {
  DropdownMenu, DropdownMenuContent, DropdownMenuItem, DropdownMenuLabel,
  DropdownMenuSeparator, DropdownMenuTrigger,
} from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/dropdown-menu";
import { Card, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/card";
import { Button } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/badge";
import { Filter, Check, X, Inbox, Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
import { apiGet, apiPatch, apiPost } from "@/lib/api";
import { useAuth } from "@/lib/auth-context";

type Reservation = {
  id: string;
  reason: string;
  numberOfParticipants: number;
  reservationStartDate: string;
  reservationEndDate: string;
  requestType: "STANDARD" | "PARTICULIER";
  userName: string;
  userPosition: string;
  eventTypeName: string;
  roomNames: string[];
};

type Room = { id: string; nameRoom: string; capacity: number };
type Filtre = "TOUS" | "STANDARD" | "PARTICULIER";

function formatCreneau(start: string, end: string): string {
  const s = new Date(start);
  const e = new Date(end);
  const day = s.toLocaleDateString("fr-FR", { day: "numeric", month: "long" });
  const t = (d: Date) => d.toLocaleTimeString("fr-FR", { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" });
  return `${day} · ${t(s)} - ${t(e)}`;
}

export default function ValidationDemandesPage() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [demandes, setDemandes] = useState<Reservation[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [filtre, setFiltre] = useState<Filtre>("TOUS");
  const [actionLoading, setActionLoading] = useState(false);

  const [approveTarget, setApproveTarget] = useState<Reservation | null>(null);
  const [denyTarget, setDenyTarget] = useState<Reservation | null>(null);
  const [denyReason, setDenyReason] = useState("");

  const [particularTarget, setParticularTarget] = useState<Reservation | null>(null);
  const [availableRooms, setAvailableRooms] = useState<Room[]>([]);
  const [selectedRoomIds, setSelectedRoomIds] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [loadingRooms, setLoadingRooms] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    apiGet<Reservation[]>("/reservations/my-site/pending")
      .then(setDemandes)
      .catch((err) => setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Erreur de chargement"))
      .finally(() => setLoading(false));
  }, []);

  const demandesFiltrees =
    filtre === "TOUS" ? demandes : demandes.filter((d) => d.requestType === filtre);

  const removeFromList = (id: string) =>
    setDemandes((prev) => prev.filter((d) => d.id !== id));

  const confirmApprove = async () => {
    if (!approveTarget) return;
    setActionLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      await apiPatch(`/reservations/${approveTarget.id}/approve`);
      removeFromList(approveTarget.id);
      setApproveTarget(null);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Échec de la validation");
    } finally {
      setActionLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const confirmDeny = async () => {
    if (!denyTarget) return;
    if (!denyReason.trim()) return setError("Le motif de refus est obligatoire");
    setActionLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      await apiPatch(`/reservations/${denyTarget.id}/deny`, denyReason.trim());
      removeFromList(denyTarget.id);
      setDenyTarget(null);
      setDenyReason("");
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Échec du refus");
    } finally {
      setActionLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const openParticular = async (demande: Reservation) => {
    setParticularTarget(demande);
    setSelectedRoomIds([]);
    setAvailableRooms([]);
    setLoadingRooms(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      const rooms = await apiGet<Room[]>(
        `/rooms/available?siteId=${user?.siteId}` +
          `&startDate=${encodeURIComponent(demande.reservationStartDate)}` +
          `&endDate=${encodeURIComponent(demande.reservationEndDate)}`
      );
      setAvailableRooms(rooms);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Impossible de charger les salles");
    } finally {
      setLoadingRooms(false);
    }
  };

  const toggleRoom = (id: string) =>
    setSelectedRoomIds((prev) =>
      prev.includes(id) ? prev.filter((r) => r !== id) : [...prev, id]
    );

  const capaciteTotale = availableRooms
    .filter((r) => selectedRoomIds.includes(r.id))
    .reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.capacity, 0);

  const capaciteSuffisante =
    particularTarget != null && capaciteTotale >= particularTarget.numberOfParticipants;

  const confirmAssign = async () => {
    if (!particularTarget) return;
    setActionLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      await apiPost(`/reservations/${particularTarget.id}/assign-rooms`, selectedRoomIds);
      removeFromList(particularTarget.id);
      setParticularTarget(null);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Échec de l'attribution");
    } finally {
      setActionLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl p-8">
      <div className="mb-8 text-center">
        <h1 className="text-3xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-[#0f2e25]">
          Validation des demandes
        </h1>
      </div>

      {error && <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-3 text-sm text-red-700">{error}</div>}

      <Card className="border-gray-200 bg-white">
        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between border-b border-gray-100">
          <CardTitle className="text-base font-semibold">Demandes en attente</CardTitle>

          <DropdownMenu>
            <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
              <Button variant="ghost" size="sm">
                <Filter className="h-4 w-4" />
              </Button>
            </DropdownMenuTrigger>
            <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="w-56">
              <DropdownMenuLabel>Filtrer par type de demande</DropdownMenuLabel>
              <DropdownMenuSeparator />
              <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => setFiltre("TOUS")}>Tous les types</DropdownMenuItem>
              <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => setFiltre("STANDARD")}>Demandes standard</DropdownMenuItem>
              <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => setFiltre("PARTICULIER")}>Demandes particulières</DropdownMenuItem>
            </DropdownMenuContent>
          </DropdownMenu>
        </CardHeader>

        {loading ? (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-16 text-sm text-gray-500">
            <Loader2 className="h-5 w-5 animate-spin" /> Chargement...
          </div>
        ) : demandesFiltrees.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-16 text-center">
            <Inbox className="h-12 w-12 text-gray-300" />
            <p className="mt-4 text-base font-medium text-gray-700">Aucune demande en attente</p>
            <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-500">Les nouvelles demandes apparaîtront ici.</p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <Table>
            <TableHeader>
              <TableRow className="border-gray-100 uppercase">
                <TableHead className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-500">Demandeur</TableHead>
                <TableHead className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-500">Salle</TableHead>
                <TableHead className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-500">Date & Créneau</TableHead>
                <TableHead className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-500">Participants</TableHead>
                <TableHead className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-500">Type</TableHead>
                <TableHead className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-500"></TableHead>
              </TableRow>
            </TableHeader>

            <TableBody>
              {demandesFiltrees.map((d) => (
                <TableRow key={d.id} className="border-gray-100">
                  <TableCell>
                    <div className="font-semibold text-[#0f2e25]">{d.userName}</div>
                    <div className="text-xs text-gray-500">{d.userPosition}</div>
                  </TableCell>

                  <TableCell className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">
                    {d.requestType === "PARTICULIER" || d.roomNames.length === 0
                      ? "À attribuer"
                      : d.roomNames.join(", ")}
                  </TableCell>

                  <TableCell className="text-sm font-medium text-[#0f2e25]">
                    {formatCreneau(d.reservationStartDate, d.reservationEndDate)}
                  </TableCell>

                  <TableCell className="text-sm text-gray-700">{d.numberOfParticipants}</TableCell>

                  <TableCell>
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                      <Badge variant="outline" className="w-fit border-gray-200 bg-gray-50 text-gray-700">
                        {d.eventTypeName}
                      </Badge>
                      <Badge
                        variant="outline"
                        className={
                          d.requestType === "PARTICULIER"
                            ? "w-fit border-purple-200 bg-purple-50 text-purple-700"
                            : "w-fit border-blue-200 bg-blue-50 text-blue-700"
                        }
                      >
                        {d.requestType === "PARTICULIER" ? "Particulière" : "Standard"}
                      </Badge>
                    </div>
                  </TableCell>

                  <TableCell>
                    <div className="flex justify-end gap-2">
                      {d.requestType === "STANDARD" ? (
                        <Button
                          size="sm"
                          className="bg-green-100 text-green-700 hover:bg-green-200"
                          onClick={() => setApproveTarget(d)}
                        >
                          <Check className="mr-1 h-4 w-4" /> Approuver
                        </Button>
                      ) : (
                        <Button
                          size="sm"
                          className="bg-green-100 text-green-700 hover:bg-green-200"
                          onClick={() => openParticular(d)}
                        >
                          <Check className="mr-1 h-4 w-4" /> Attribuer salles
                        </Button>
                      )}
                      <Button
                        size="sm"
                        className="bg-red-100 text-red-700 hover:bg-red-200"
                        onClick={() => setDenyTarget(d)}
                      >
                        <X className="mr-1 h-4 w-4" /> Refuser
                      </Button>
                    </div>
                  </TableCell>
                </TableRow>
              ))}
            </TableBody>
          </Table>
        )}
      </Card>

      {approveTarget && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/40 p-4">
          <div className="w-full max-w-md rounded-xl bg-white p-6 text-center shadow-xl">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-[#0f2e25]">Valider cette réservation ?</h3>
            <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-gray-600">
              Confirmez-vous la validation de la demande de {approveTarget.userName} ?
            </p>
            <div className="mt-6 flex justify-center gap-2">
              <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setApproveTarget(null)} disabled={actionLoading}>
                Non
              </Button>
              <Button
                onClick={confirmApprove}
                disabled={actionLoading}
                className="bg-[#0F2E25] text-white hover:bg-[#0F2E25]/90"
              >
                {actionLoading ? "..." : "Oui"}
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {denyTarget && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/40 p-4">
          <div className="w-full max-w-md rounded-xl bg-white p-6 shadow-xl">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-[#0f2e25]">Refuser la demande</h3>
            <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-600">Indiquez le motif du refus :</p>
            <textarea
              value={denyReason}
              onChange={(e) => setDenyReason(e.target.value)}
              rows={3}
              placeholder="Salle indisponible, créneau réservé..."
              className="mt-3 w-full rounded-md border border-gray-300 px-3 py-2 text-sm outline-none focus:border-[#0F2E25]"
            />
            <div className="mt-6 flex justify-end gap-2">
              <Button
                variant="outline"
                onClick={() => { setDenyTarget(null); setDenyReason(""); }}
                disabled={actionLoading}
              >
                Annuler
              </Button>
              <Button
                onClick={confirmDeny}
                disabled={actionLoading}
                className="bg-red-600 text-white hover:bg-red-700"
              >
                {actionLoading ? "..." : "Confirmer le refus"}
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {particularTarget && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/40 p-4">
          <div className="w-full max-w-lg rounded-xl bg-white p-6 shadow-xl">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-[#0f2e25]">Attribuer des salles</h3>
            <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-600">
              Sélectionnez des salles jusqu'à atteindre {particularTarget.numberOfParticipants} places.
            </p>

            <div className="mt-4 max-h-72 space-y-2 overflow-y-auto">
              {loadingRooms ? (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 py-6 text-sm text-gray-500">
                  <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" /> Chargement des salles...
                </div>
              ) : availableRooms.length === 0 ? (
                <p className="py-6 text-sm text-gray-500">Aucune salle libre sur ce créneau.</p>
              ) : (
                availableRooms.map((room) => {
                  const checked = selectedRoomIds.includes(room.id);
                  return (
                    <button
                      key={room.id}
                      type="button"
                      onClick={() => toggleRoom(room.id)}
                      className={`flex w-full items-center justify-between rounded-lg border px-4 py-3 text-left text-sm ${
                        checked ? "border-[#0F2E25] bg-[#0F2E25]/5" : "border-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-50"
                      }`}
                    >
                      <span className="font-medium text-gray-800">{room.nameRoom}</span>
                      <span className="text-gray-500">{room.capacity} places</span>
                    </button>
                  );
                })
              )}
            </div>

            <div className="mt-4 rounded-lg bg-gray-50 p-3 text-sm">
              Capacité sélectionnée :{" "}
              <span className={capaciteSuffisante ? "font-semibold text-green-700" : "font-semibold text-red-600"}>
                {capaciteTotale}
              </span>{" "}
              / {particularTarget.numberOfParticipants} requis
            </div>

            <div className="mt-6 flex justify-end gap-2">
              <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setParticularTarget(null)} disabled={actionLoading}>
                Annuler
              </Button>
              <Button
                onClick={confirmAssign}
                disabled={actionLoading || !capaciteSuffisante}
                className="bg-[#0F2E25] text-white hover:bg-[#0F2E25]/90"
              >
                {actionLoading ? "..." : "Valider"}
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

\n\n=== FILENAME: src/app/espace/gestion-salles/nouvelle-salle/page.tsx ===
"use client";

import { useState, useRef } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { Upload, X, Image as ImageIcon, Loader2 } from "lucide-react";

import {
  Card,
  CardContent,
  CardHeader,
  CardTitle,
  CardDescription,
} from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/card";
import { Input } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/input";
import { Label } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/label";
import { Button } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/button";

import { apiPost } from "@/lib/api";


type RoomRequest = {
  nameRoom: string;
  capacity: number;
  siteId?: string;
  equipmentsId: string[];
};


export default function NouvelleSallePage() {
  const router = useRouter();

  const [nameRoom, setNameRoom] = useState("");
  const [capacity, setCapacity] = useState<number | "">("");


  const [imageFile, setImageFile] = useState<File | null>(null);
  const [imagePreview, setImagePreview] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [imageError, setImageError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);

  
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  
  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  // ============================================================
  // GESTION DE L'IMAGE
  // ============================================================

  // Valider et traiter le fichier sélectionné
  const handleFile = (file: File) => {
    // Validation : type
    if (!file.type.startsWith("image/")) {
      setImageError("Le fichier doit être une image (PNG ou JPG)");
      return;
    }

    // Validation : taille (5 MB max)
    if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
      setImageError("L'image ne doit pas dépasser 5 MB");
      return;
    }

    setImageError(null);
    setImageFile(file);

    // Créer une prévisualisation
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onloadend = () => {
      setImagePreview(reader.result as string);
    };
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  };

  // Sélection via le bouton "Sélectionner une image"
  const handleFileSelect = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (file) handleFile(file);
  };

  // Glisser-déposer : entrée
  const handleDragOver = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setIsDragging(true);
  };

  // Glisser-déposer : sortie
  const handleDragLeave = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setIsDragging(false);
  };

  // Glisser-déposer : dépôt
  const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setIsDragging(false);
    const file = e.dataTransfer.files?.[0];
    if (file) handleFile(file);
  };

  // Supprimer l'image
  const removeImage = () => {
    setImageFile(null);
    setImagePreview(null);
    setImageError(null);
    if (fileInputRef.current) {
      fileInputRef.current.value = "";
    }
  };

  // ============================================================
  // SOUMISSION DU FORMULAIRE
  // ============================================================
const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    if (!nameRoom.trim()) {
      setError("Le nom de la salle est obligatoire");
      return;
    }
    if (!capacity || capacity < 1) {
      setError("La capacité doit être au moins de 1 personne");
      return;
    }

    setSubmitting(true);
    setError(null);

    try {
      const roomData: RoomRequest = {
        nameRoom: nameRoom.trim(),
        capacity: Number(capacity),
        equipmentsId: [],
      };

      await apiPost("/rooms", roomData);
      router.push("/espace/gestion-salles");
    } catch (err) {
      setError(
        err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Erreur lors de la création de la salle"
      );
    } finally {
      setSubmitting(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="mx-auto max-w-4xl space-y-6">
      {/* ===== EN-TÊTE ===== */}
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-[var(--bni-text)]">
          Nouvelle salle
        </h1>
        <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          Ajoutez une nouvelle salle à votre site
        </p>
      </div>

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-6">
        <Card>
          <CardHeader>
            <CardTitle>Informations de la salle</CardTitle>
            <CardDescription>
              Renseignez les caractéristiques principales de la salle.
            </CardDescription>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent className="space-y-4">
            {/* Nom de la salle */}
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="nameRoom" className="text-sm font-medium">
                Nom de la salle
              </Label>
              <Input
                id="nameRoom"
                type="text"
                placeholder="Ex : CARDLESS, B.FREE, Salle de conférence..."
                value={nameRoom}
                onChange={(e) => setNameRoom(e.target.value)}

                Choisissez un nom unique et facilement identifiable.
              </p>
            </div>

            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="capacity" className="text-sm font-medium">
                Capacité (nombre de personnes)
              </Label>
              <Input
                id="capacity"
                type="number"
                min="1"
                placeholder="Ex : 20"
                value={capacity}
                onChange={(e) =>
                  setCapacity(
                    e.target.value === "" ? "" : Number(e.target.value)
                  )
                }
                disabled={submitting}
                className="max-w-[200px]"
              />
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                Nombre maximum de personnes que la salle peut accueillir.
              </p>
            </div>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
        <Card>
          <CardHeader>
            <CardTitle>Photos de la salle</CardTitle>
            <CardDescription>
              Ajoutez des photos pour aider les utilisateurs à reconnaître la salle.
            </CardDescription>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent>
            {/* Si une image est sélectionnée → afficher la prévisualisation */}
            {imagePreview ? (
              <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-lg border border-border">
                {/* eslint-disable-next-line @next/next/no-img-element */}
                <img
                  src={imagePreview}
                  alt="Prévisualisation"
                  className="h-64 w-full object-cover"
                />

                  type="button"
                  onClick={removeImage}
                  className="absolute right-2 top-2 rounded-full bg-black/60 p-1.5 text-white transition hover:bg-black/80"
                  aria-label="Supprimer l'image"
                >
                  <X className="h-4 w-4" />
                </button>
              </div>

                onDragOver={handleDragOver}
                onDragLeave={handleDragLeave}
                onDrop={handleDrop}

                  isDragging
                    ? "border-[var(--bni-main)] bg-[var(--bni-main)]/5"
                    : "border-border bg-gray-50/50"

                  <Upload className="h-4 w-4" />

                <input
                  ref={fileInputRef}
                  type="file"
                  accept="image/png,image/jpeg"
                  onChange={handleFileSelect}
                  className="hidden"
                />
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Message d'erreur sur l'image */}
            {imageError && (
              <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-red-600">{imageError}</p>
            )}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* ===== MESSAGE D'ERREUR GLOBAL ===== */}
        {error && (
          <div className="rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-3 text-sm text-red-700">
            {error}

                Création...
              </>
            ) : (
              "Créer la salle"
            )}
          </Button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  );

"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";
import { Button } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/button";
import { Plus, Home, Users, Lock, Unlock, Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
import { apiGet, apiPatch } from "@/lib/api";
import { useAuth } from "@/lib/auth-context";

type Salle = {
  id: string;
  nameRoom: string;
  capacity: number;
  isBlocked: boolean;
  siteId: string | null;
  siteName: string | null;
};

export default function GestionSallesPage() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [salles, setSalles] = useState<Salle[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [selectedSiteId, setSelectedSiteId] = useState("");

  const estAdminSite = user?.roleName === "ADMIN_SITE";
  const estSuperAdmin = user?.roleName === "SUPER_ADMIN";

  useEffect(() => {
    apiGet<Salle[]>("/rooms")
      .then(setSalles)
      .catch((err) => setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Erreur de chargement"))
      .finally(() => setLoading(false));
  }, []);

  const sites = Array.from(
    new Map(
      salles
        .filter((s) => s.siteId)
        .map((s) => [s.siteId, { id: s.siteId as string, name: s.siteName ?? "—" }])
    ).values()
  );

  const sallesAffichees = selectedSiteId
    ? salles.filter((s) => s.siteId === selectedSiteId)
    : salles;

  const toggleBlock = async (id: string) => {
    const previous = salles;
    setSalles((prev) =>
      prev.map((s) => (s.id === id ? { ...s, isBlocked: !s.isBlocked } : s))
    );
    try {
      await apiPatch(`/rooms/${id}/lockRoom`);
    } catch (err) {
      setSalles(previous);
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Échec du changement");
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl p-8">
      <div className="mb-8 flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-[#0f2e25]">Salles</h1>
          <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-gray-600">Liste des salles</p>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          {estSuperAdmin && sites.length > 0 && (
            <select
              value={selectedSiteId}
              onChange={(e) => setSelectedSiteId(e.target.value)}
              className="rounded-lg border border-gray-300 bg-white px-3 py-2 text-sm text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-[#0F2E25]"
            >
              <option value="">Tous les sites</option>
              {sites.map((site) => (
                <option key={site.id} value={site.id}>
                  {site.name}
                </option>
              ))}
            </select>
          )}

          {estAdminSite && (
            <Link href="/espace/gestion-salles/nouvelle-salle">
              <Button className="bg-[var(--bni-main)] text-white hover:bg-[var(--bni-main)]/90">
                <Plus className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
                Ajouter une salle
              </Button>
            </Link>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {error && <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-3 text-sm text-red-700">{error}</div>}

      {loading ? (
        <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-20 text-sm text-gray-500">
          <Loader2 className="h-5 w-5 animate-spin" /> Chargement des salles...
        </div>
      ) : salles.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="rounded-lg border border-gray-200 bg-white">
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center px-6 py-20 text-center">
            <div className="mb-4 flex h-16 w-16 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-gray-100">
              <Home className="h-8 w-8 text-gray-500" />
            </div>
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">Pas encore de salles</h2>
            <p className="mt-2 max-w-sm text-sm text-gray-600">
              Aucune salle n'a encore été créée.
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>
      ) : sallesAffichees.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="rounded-lg border border-gray-200 bg-white px-6 py-16 text-center">
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Aucune salle pour ce site.</p>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-6 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3">
          {sallesAffichees.map((salle) => (
            <div
              key={salle.id}
              className="overflow-hidden rounded-xl border border-gray-200 bg-white shadow-sm"
            >
              <div className="relative flex h-44 w-full items-center justify-center bg-gray-100">
                <Home className="h-10 w-10 text-gray-400" />
                {salle.isBlocked && (
                  <span className="absolute right-3 top-3 rounded-full bg-red-600 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-white">
                    Bloquée
                  </span>
                )}
              </div>

              <div className="p-4">
                <h3 className="text-base font-semibold text-gray-900">{salle.nameRoom}</h3>
                <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500">{salle.siteName ?? "—"}</p>

                <div className="mt-3 flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-gray-600">
                  <Users className="h-4 w-4" />
                  {salle.capacity} personnes
                </div>

                <Button
                  variant="outline"
                  className="mt-4 w-full"
                  onClick={() => toggleBlock(salle.id)}
                >
                  {salle.isBlocked ? (
                    <>
                      <Unlock className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Débloquer
                    </>
                  ) : (
                    <>
                      <Lock className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> Bloquer
                    </>
                  )}
                </Button>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );

"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/button";
import { CalendarPlus, ArrowLeft } from "lucide-react";
import { apiGet } from "@/lib/api";
import ReservationSearchBar, { SearchCriteria } from "./_components/ReservationSearchBar";
import RoomResults, { Room } from "./_components/RoomResults";
import RoomCalendar from "./_components/RoomCalendar";
import ReservationList from "./_components/ReservationList";

type Step = "list" | "search" | "calendar";
type Mode = "STANDARD" | "PARTICULIER";

export default function MesReservationsPage() {
  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>("list");
  const [mode, setMode] = useState<Mode>("STANDARD");
  const [criteria, setCriteria] = useState<SearchCriteria | null>(null);
  const [rooms, setRooms] = useState<Room[]>([]);
  const [hasSearched, setHasSearched] = useState(false);
  const [selectedRoom, setSelectedRoom] = useState<Room | null>(null);
  const [showParticulier, setShowParticulier] = useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const openSearch = () => {
    setRooms([]);
    setCriteria(null);
    setHasSearched(false);
    setError(null);
    setStep("search");
  };

  const handleSearch = async (c: SearchCriteria) => {
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      const data = await apiGet<Room[]>(
        `/rooms/bookable?siteId=${c.siteId}&participants=${c.participants}`
      );
      setCriteria(c);
      setRooms(data);
      setHasSearched(true);
      if (data.length === 0) {
        setShowParticulier(true);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Erreur de recherche");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const confirmParticulier = () => {
    setShowParticulier(false);
    setSelectedRoom(null);
    setMode("PARTICULIER");
    setStep("calendar");
  };

  return (
    <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl p-8">
      <div className="mb-8 flex items-start justify-between gap-4">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-[#0f2e25]">Mes réservations</h1>
          <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-gray-600">Consultez et gérez vos réservations</p>
        </div>

        {step === "list" ? (
          <Button onClick={openSearch} className="bg-[var(--bni-main)] text-white hover:bg-[var(--bni-main)]/90">
            <CalendarPlus className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
            Faire une réservation
          </Button>
        ) : (
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            onClick={() => setStep(step === "calendar" ? "search" : "list")}
          >
            <ArrowLeft className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
            Retour
          </Button>
        )}
      </div>

      {error && <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-3 text-sm text-red-700">{error}</div>}

      {step === "list" && <ReservationList />}

      {step === "search" && (
        <div className="space-y-8">
          <ReservationSearchBar onSearch={handleSearch} loading={loading} />

          {hasSearched && criteria && rooms.length > 0 && (
            <div>
              <p className="mb-6 text-sm text-gray-600">
                {criteria.siteName} ·{" "}
                {new Date(criteria.date).toLocaleDateString("fr-FR")} ·{" "}
                {criteria.participants} participant(s)
              </p>
              <RoomResults
                rooms={rooms}
                onViewRoom={(room) => {
                  setSelectedRoom(room);
                  setMode("STANDARD");
                  setStep("calendar");
                }}
              />
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {step === "calendar" && criteria && (
        <RoomCalendar
          room={mode === "STANDARD" ? selectedRoom : null}
          requestType={mode}
          siteId={criteria.siteId}
          participants={criteria.participants}
          initialDate={criteria.date}
          onBooked={() => setStep("list")}
        />
      )}

      {showParticulier && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/40 p-4">
          <div className="w-full max-w-md rounded-xl bg-white p-6 text-center shadow-xl">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-[#0f2e25]">Aucune salle disponible</h3>
            <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-gray-600">
              Aucune salle ne correspond à cette demande. Voulez-vous faire une demande particulière ?
            </p>
            <div className="mt-6 flex justify-center gap-2">
              <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowParticulier(false)}>
                Annuler
              </Button>
              <Button onClick={confirmParticulier} className="bg-[#0F2E25] text-white hover:bg-[#0F2E25]/90">
                Soumettre demande
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}


\n\n=== FILENAME: src/app/espace/mes-reservations/_components/ReservationList.tsx ===
"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { Calendar, Users, MapPin, Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
import { Button } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/badge";
import { apiGet, apiPatch } from "@/lib/api";

type Reservation = {
  id: string;
  reason: string;
  numberOfParticipants: number;
  reservationStartDate: string;
  reservationEndDate: string;
  status: "EN_ATTENTE" | "VALIDEE" | "REFUSEE" | "ANNULEE";
  requestType: "STANDARD" | "PARTICULIER";
  denialReason: string | null;
  eventTypeName: string;
  roomNames: string[];
};

const statusStyles: Record<Reservation["status"], { label: string; className: string }> = {
  EN_ATTENTE: { label: "En attente", className: "border-amber-200 bg-amber-50 text-amber-700" },
  VALIDEE: { label: "Validée", className: "border-emerald-200 bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-700" },
  REFUSEE: { label: "Refusée", className: "border-red-200 bg-red-50 text-red-700" },
  ANNULEE: { label: "Annulée", className: "border-gray-200 bg-gray-100 text-gray-600" },
};

function formatRange(start: string, end: string): string {
  const s = new Date(start);
  const e = new Date(end);
  const day = s.toLocaleDateString("fr-FR", { weekday: "long", day: "2-digit", month: "long" });
  const time = (d: Date) => d.toLocaleTimeString("fr-FR", { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" });
  return `${day} · ${time(s)} → ${time(e)}`;
}

export default function ReservationList() {
  const [reservations, setReservations] = useState<Reservation[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [cancelingId, setCancelingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [info, setInfo] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    apiGet<Reservation[]>("/reservations/me")
      .then(setReservations)
      .catch((err) => setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Erreur de chargement"))
      .finally(() => setLoading(false));
  }, []);

  const handleCancel = async (id: string) => {
    setCancelingId(id);
    setError(null);
    try {
      await apiPatch(`/reservations/${id}/cancel`);
      setReservations((prev) => prev.filter((r) => r.id !== id));
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Échec de l'annulation");
    } finally {
      setCancelingId(null);
    }
  };

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-20 text-sm text-gray-500">
        <Loader2 className="h-5 w-5 animate-spin" />
        Chargement de vos réservations...
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (reservations.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="rounded-lg border border-gray-200 bg-white">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center px-6 py-20 text-center">
          <div className="mb-4 flex h-16 w-16 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-gray-100">
            <Calendar className="h-8 w-8 text-gray-500" />
          </div>
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">Pas encore de réservations</h2>
          <p className="mt-2 max-w-sm text-sm text-gray-600">
            Cliquez sur « Faire une réservation » pour rechercher une salle disponible.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div>
      {error && <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-3 text-sm text-red-700">{error}</div>}
      {info && <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg bg-blue-50 p-3 text-sm text-blue-700">{info}</div>}

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-5 lg:grid-cols-2">
        {reservations.map((r) => {
          const badge = statusStyles[r.status];
          const canCancel = r.status === "EN_ATTENTE" || r.status === "VALIDEE";
          const rooms =
            r.requestType === "PARTICULIER" || r.roomNames.length === 0
              ? "Demande particulière (salles à attribuer)"
              : r.roomNames.join(", ");

          return (
            <div key={r.id} className="flex flex-col rounded-xl border border-gray-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                <h3 className="text-base font-semibold text-[#0f2e25]">{r.eventTypeName}</h3>
                <Badge variant="outline" className={badge.className}>{badge.label}</Badge>
              </div>

              <div className="mt-3 space-y-2 text-sm text-gray-600">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 flex-shrink-0 text-gray-400" />
                  {rooms}
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <Calendar className="h-4 w-4 flex-shrink-0 text-gray-400" />
                  {formatRange(r.reservationStartDate, r.reservationEndDate)}
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <Users className="h-4 w-4 flex-shrink-0 text-gray-400" />
                  {r.numberOfParticipants} participant(s)
                </div>
              </div>

              {r.reason && <p className="mt-3 text-sm italic text-gray-500">« {r.reason} »</p>}

              {r.status === "REFUSEE" && r.denialReason && (
                <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-red-600">Motif du refus : {r.denialReason}</p>
              )}

              <div className="mt-4 flex gap-2 border-t border-gray-100 pt-4">
                <Button
                  variant="outline"
                  className="flex-1"
                  onClick={() => setInfo("La modification sera bientôt disponible.")}
                >
                  Modifier
                </Button>
                <Button
                  variant="outline"
                  className="flex-1 border-red-200 text-red-600 hover:bg-red-50 hover:text-red-700"
                  disabled={!canCancel || cancelingId === r.id}
                  onClick={() => handleCancel(r.id)}
                >
                  {cancelingId === r.id ? "Annulation..." : "Annuler"}
                </Button>
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}\n\n=== FILENAME: src/app/espace/mes-reservations/_components/ReservationSearchBar.tsx ===
"use client";

import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import { MapPin, CalendarDays, Users, Search } from "lucide-react";
import { format } from "date-fns";
import { fr } from "date-fns/locale";
import { Button } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/button";
import { Calendar } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/calendar";
import {
  Popover,
  PopoverContent,
  PopoverTrigger,
} from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/popover";
import { apiGet } from "@/lib/api";

type SiteOption = { id: string; nameSite: string };

export type SearchCriteria = {
  siteId: string;
  siteName: string;
  date: string;
  participants: number;
};

export default function ReservationSearchBar({
  onSearch,
  loading,
}: {
  onSearch: (criteria: SearchCriteria) => void;
  loading: boolean;
}) {
  const [sites, setSites] = useState<SiteOption[]>([]);
  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
  const [selectedSite, setSelectedSite] = useState<SiteOption | null>(null);
  const [showResults, setShowResults] = useState(false);
  const [dateValue, setDateValue] = useState<Date | undefined>(undefined);
  const [dateOpen, setDateOpen] = useState(false);
  const [participants, setParticipants] = useState(2);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const boxRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const startOfToday = new Date();
  startOfToday.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

  useEffect(() => {
    apiGet<SiteOption[]>("/sites/actives")
      .then(setSites)
      .catch(() => setError("Impossible de charger les sites"));
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    function handleClickOutside(e: MouseEvent) {
      if (boxRef.current && !boxRef.current.contains(e.target as Node)) {
        setShowResults(false);
      }
    }
    document.addEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
  }, []);

  const matches = query.trim()
    ? sites.filter((s) =>
        s.nameSite.toLowerCase().includes(query.trim().toLowerCase())
      )
    : sites;

  const handleQueryChange = (value: string) => {
    setQuery(value);
    setSelectedSite(null);
    setShowResults(true);
  };

  const handleSelectSite = (site: SiteOption) => {
    setSelectedSite(site);
    setQuery(site.nameSite);
    setShowResults(false);
  };

  const handleSubmit = () => {
    if (!selectedSite) return setError("Choisissez un lieu dans la liste des suggestions");
    if (!dateValue) return setError("Choisissez une date");
    if (dateValue < startOfToday) return setError("La date ne peut pas être dans le passé");
    if (!participants || participants < 1)
      return setError("Le nombre de participants doit être au moins 1");
    setError(null);
    onSearch({
      siteId: selectedSite.id,
      siteName: selectedSite.nameSite,
      date: format(dateValue, "yyyy-MM-dd"),
      participants,
    });
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="flex flex-col items-stretch gap-2 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 bg-white p-2 shadow-sm md:flex-row md:items-center md:rounded-full">
        <div ref={boxRef} className="relative flex-1">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2">
            <MapPin className="h-5 w-5 flex-shrink-0 text-gray-400" />
            <input
              type="text"
              value={query}
              onChange={(e) => handleQueryChange(e.target.value)}
              onFocus={() => setShowResults(true)}
              placeholder="Où aura lieu l'événement ?"
              className="w-full bg-transparent text-sm text-gray-700 outline-none"
            />
          </div>

          {showResults && (
            <div className="absolute left-0 right-0 top-full z-20 mt-2 max-h-60 overflow-y-auto rounded-xl border border-gray-200 bg-white py-1 shadow-lg">
              {matches.length === 0 ? (
                <p className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-500">Aucun site trouvé</p>
              ) : (
                matches.map((s) => (
                  <button
                    key={s.id}
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => handleSelectSite(s)}
                    className="flex w-full items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-100"
                  >
                    <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 flex-shrink-0 text-gray-400" />
                    {s.nameSite}
                  </button>
                ))
              )}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="hidden h-8 w-px bg-gray-200 md:block" />

        <Popover open={dateOpen} onOpenChange={setDateOpen}>
          <PopoverTrigger asChild>
            <button
              type="button"
              className="flex flex-1 items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm outline-none"
            >
              <CalendarDays className="h-5 w-5 flex-shrink-0 text-gray-400" />
              <span className={dateValue ? "text-gray-700" : "text-gray-400"}>
                {dateValue
                  ? format(dateValue, "d MMM yyyy", { locale: fr })
                  : "Date de l'événement"}
              </span>
            </button>
          </PopoverTrigger>
          <PopoverContent className="w-auto p-0" align="start">
            <Calendar
              mode="single"
              selected={dateValue}
              onSelect={(d) => {
                setDateValue(d);
                setDateOpen(false);
                setError(null);
              }}
              disabled={{ before: startOfToday }}
              locale={fr}
            />
          </PopoverContent>
        </Popover>

        <div className="hidden h-8 w-px bg-gray-200 md:block" />

        <div className="flex flex-1 items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2">
          <Users className="h-5 w-5 flex-shrink-0 text-gray-400" />
          <input
            type="number"
            min={1}
            value={participants}
            onChange={(e) => setParticipants(Number(e.target.value))}
            className="w-16 bg-transparent text-sm text-gray-700 outline-none"
          />
          <span className="whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-500">participants</span>
        </div>

        <Button
          onClick={handleSubmit}
          disabled={loading}
          className="rounded-full bg-[#0F2E25] px-6 text-white hover:bg-[#0F2E25]/90"
        >
          <Search className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
          {loading ? "Recherche..." : "Rechercher"}
        </Button>
      </div>

      {error && <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-red-600">{error}</p>}
    </div>
  );
}\n\n=== FILENAME: src/app/espace/mes-reservations/_components/RoomCalendar.tsx ===
"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import FullCalendar from "@fullcalendar/react";
import timeGridPlugin from "@fullcalendar/timegrid";
import interactionPlugin from "@fullcalendar/interaction";
import frLocale from "@fullcalendar/core/locales/fr";
import { Button } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/button";
import { apiGet, apiPost } from "@/lib/api";
import { Room } from "./RoomResults";

type ValidatedReservation = {
  id: string;
  reservationStartDate: string;
  reservationEndDate: string;
};

type EventType = { id: string; eventTypeName: string };

type RequestType = "STANDARD" | "PARTICULIER";

function toLocalDateTime(d: Date): string {
  const pad = (n: number) => String(n).padStart(2, "0");
  return `${d.getFullYear()}-${pad(d.getMonth() + 1)}-${pad(d.getDate())}T${pad(d.getHours())}:${pad(d.getMinutes())}:00`;
}

export default function RoomCalendar({
  room,
  requestType,
  siteId,
  participants,
  initialDate,
  onBooked,
}: {
  room: Room | null;
  requestType: RequestType;
  siteId: string;
  participants: number;
  initialDate: string;
  onBooked: () => void;
}) {
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState<{ start: string; end: string }[]>([]);
  const [eventTypes, setEventTypes] = useState<EventType[]>([]);
  const [selection, setSelection] = useState<{ start: string; end: string } | null>(null);
  const [reason, setReason] = useState("");
  const [eventTypeId, setEventTypeId] = useState("");
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (requestType === "STANDARD" && room) {
      apiGet<ValidatedReservation[]>(`/reservations/rooms/validated?roomIds=${room.id}`)
        .then((data) =>
          setBusy(data.map((r) => ({ start: r.reservationStartDate, end: r.reservationEndDate })))
        )
        .catch(() => setError("Impossible de charger les créneaux occupés"));
    }
    apiGet<EventType[]>("/event-types").then(setEventTypes).catch(() => {});
  }, [room, requestType]);

  const events = busy.map((b) => ({
    title: "Occupé",
    start: b.start,
    end: b.end,
    backgroundColor: "#dc2626",
    borderColor: "#dc2626",
  }));

  const handleConfirm = async () => {
    if (!selection) return;
    if (!eventTypeId) return setError("Choisissez un type d'événement");
    if (!reason.trim()) return setError("Indiquez le motif");

    setSubmitting(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      await apiPost("/reservations", {
        reason: reason.trim(),
        numberOfParticipants: participants,
        reservationStartDate: selection.start,
        reservationEndDate: selection.end,
        requestType,
        siteId,
        eventTypeId,
        roomIds: requestType === "STANDARD" && room ? [room.id] : [],
      });
      onBooked();
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Échec de la réservation");
    } finally {
      setSubmitting(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="mb-4">
        <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-[#0f2e25]">
          {requestType === "PARTICULIER" ? "Demande particulière" : room?.nameRoom}
        </h2>
        {requestType === "PARTICULIER" ? (
          <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-600">
             Choisissez votre créneau , un administrateur vous attribuera les salles.
          </p>
        ) : (
          <p className="mt-1 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-4 text-sm text-gray-600">
            <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
              <span className="inline-block h-3 w-3 rounded-sm bg-red-600" /> Occupé
            </span>
            <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
              <span className="inline-block h-3 w-3 rounded-sm bg-green-500" /> Libre — cliquez-glissez pour réserver
            </span>
          </p>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="rounded-lg border border-gray-200 bg-white p-4 shadow-sm">
        <style>{`.fc .fc-highlight { background: rgba(34,197,94,0.30); }`}</style>
        <FullCalendar
          plugins={[timeGridPlugin, interactionPlugin]}
          initialView="timeGridWeek"
          initialDate={initialDate}
          locale={frLocale}
          firstDay={1}
          headerToolbar={{ left: "prev,next today", center: "title", right: "" }}
          buttonText={{ today: "Aujourd'hui" }}
          slotMinTime="07:00:00"
          slotMaxTime="19:00:00"
          allDaySlot={false}
          weekends={false}
          height="auto"
          selectable={true}
          selectMirror={true}
          selectOverlap={false}
          selectAllow={(info) => info.start >= new Date()}
          events={events}
          select={(info) => {
            setSelection({ start: toLocalDateTime(info.start), end: toLocalDateTime(info.end) });
            setError(null);
          }}
        />
      </div>

      {selection && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/40 p-4">
          <div className="w-full max-w-md rounded-xl bg-white p-6 shadow-xl">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-[#0f2e25]">Confirmer la réservation</h3>
            <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-600">
              {requestType === "PARTICULIER" ? "Demande particulière" : room?.nameRoom} ·{" "}
              {new Date(selection.start).toLocaleString("fr-FR")} →{" "}
              {new Date(selection.end).toLocaleTimeString("fr-FR", { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" })}
            </p>

            <div className="mt-4 space-y-3">
              <div>
                <label className="mb-1 block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">Type d'événement</label>
                <select
                  value={eventTypeId}
                  onChange={(e) => setEventTypeId(e.target.value)}
                  className="w-full rounded-md border border-gray-300 px-3 py-2 text-sm outline-none focus:border-[#0F2E25]"
                >
                  <option value="">Choisir...</option>
                  {eventTypes.map((et) => (
                    <option key={et.id} value={et.id}>{et.eventTypeName}</option>
                  ))}
                </select>
              </div>

              <div>
                <label className="mb-1 block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">Motif</label>
                <textarea
                  value={reason}
                  onChange={(e) => setReason(e.target.value)}
                  rows={3}
                  placeholder="Réunion d'équipe, séminaire..."
                  className="w-full rounded-md border border-gray-300 px-3 py-2 text-sm outline-none focus:border-[#0F2E25]"
                />
              </div>
            </div>

            {error && <p className="mt-3 text-sm text-red-600">{error}</p>}

            <div className="mt-6 flex justify-end gap-2">
              <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setSelection(null)} disabled={submitting}>
                Annuler
              </Button>
              <Button
                onClick={handleConfirm}
                disabled={submitting}
                className="bg-[#0F2E25] text-white hover:bg-[#0F2E25]/90"
              >
                {submitting ? "Envoi..." : "Confirmer"}
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}\n\n=== FILENAME: src/app/espace/mes-reservations/_components/RoomResults.tsx ===
"use client";

import { Home, Users } from "lucide-react";
import { Button } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/button";

export type Room = {
  id: string;
  nameRoom: string;
  capacity: number;
  isBlocked: boolean;
  siteName: string | null;
};

export default function RoomResults({
  rooms,
  onViewRoom,
}: {
  rooms: Room[];
  onViewRoom: (room: Room) => void;
}) {
  if (rooms.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="rounded-lg border border-gray-200 bg-white px-6 py-16 text-center">
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Aucune salle disponible.</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="mb-8 text-center">
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-[#0f2e25]">Salles</h2>
        <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-500">liste des salles</p>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-x-10 gap-y-12 sm:grid-cols-2">
        {rooms.map((room) => (
          <div key={room.id} className="flex flex-col">
            <div className="flex h-52 w-full items-center justify-center rounded-md bg-gray-100">
              <Home className="h-10 w-10 text-gray-400" />
            </div>

            <h3 className="mt-4 text-lg font-bold italic text-[#0f2e25]">
              {room.nameRoom}
            </h3>

            <div className="mt-1 flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-semibold text-gray-700">
              <Users className="h-4 w-4" />
              {room.capacity}
            </div>

            <Button
              onClick={() => onViewRoom(room)}
              className="mt-4 self-start rounded-md bg-[#436851] px-10 font-semibold uppercase tracking-wide text-white hover:bg-[#436851]/90"
            >
              Voir salle
            </Button>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );

"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { format } from "date-fns";
import { fr } from "date-fns/locale";
import { CalendarIcon, Building2, Sparkles } from "lucide-react";

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
import { Button } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/button";
import { Input } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/input";
import { Label } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/label";
import { Textarea } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/textarea";
import {
  Card,
  CardContent,
  CardDescription,
  CardHeader,
  CardTitle,
} from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/card";
import {
  Select,
  SelectContent,
  SelectItem,
  SelectTrigger,
  SelectValue,
} from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/select";
import {
  Popover,
  PopoverContent,
  PopoverTrigger,
} from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/popover";
import { Calendar } from "@/components/template/shadcnblocs/calendar";

type RequestType = "STANDARD" | "PARTICULIER";

export default function NouvelleReservationPage() {
  const router = useRouter();

  // ===== ÉTAT DU FORMULAIRE =====
  const [requestType, setRequestType] = useState<RequestType>("STANDARD");
  const [reason, setReason] = useState("");
  const [eventTypeId, setEventTypeId] = useState("");
  const [numberOfParticipants, setNumberOfParticipants] = useState<number | "">("");
  const [date, setDate] = useState<Date | undefined>(undefined);
  const [startTime, setStartTime] = useState("");
  const [endTime, setEndTime] = useState("");
  const [precisions, setPrecisions] = useState("");
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);

  // ===== HEURES DISPONIBLES (7h - 19h, créneaux de 30 min) =====
  const horaires: string[] = [];
  for (let h = 7; h <= 19; h++) {
    horaires.push(`${String(h).padStart(2, "0")}:00`);
    if (h < 19) horaires.push(`${String(h).padStart(2, "0")}:30`);
  }

  // ===== RECHERCHE DE SALLES =====
  const handleChercherSalles = async () => {
    if (!date || !startTime || !endTime || !reason || !eventTypeId || !numberOfParticipants) {
      alert("Veuillez remplir tous les champs obligatoires");
      return;
    }

    setSubmitting(true);
    try {
      // Construire les LocalDateTime à partir de la date + heures
      const dateStr = format(date, "yyyy-MM-dd");
      const startDateTime = `${dateStr}T${startTime}:00`;
      const endDateTime = `${dateStr}T${endTime}:00`;

      // Stocker les données du formulaire pour la page suivante
      const formData = {
        reason,
        eventTypeId,
        numberOfParticipants: Number(numberOfParticipants),
        reservationStartDate: startDateTime,
        reservationEndDate: endDateTime,
        precisions,
        requestType,
      };

      sessionStorage.setItem("reservationDraft", JSON.stringify(formData));

      if (requestType === "STANDARD") {
        router.push("/espace/nouvelle-reservation/chercher-salles");
      } else {
        router.push("/espace/nouvelle-reservation/confirmation");
      }
    } finally {
      setSubmitting(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="mx-auto max-w-4xl space-y-6 p-6">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-[var(--bni-text)]">
          Nouvelle réservation
        </h1>
        <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          Remplissez le formulaire pour soumettre votre demande
        </p>
      </div>

  
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 md:grid-cols-2">
        <Card
          onClick={() => setRequestType("STANDARD")}
          className={cn(
            "cursor-pointer transition-all hover:ring-foreground/20",
            requestType === "STANDARD" &&
              "ring-2 ring-[var(--bni-main)] bg-[var(--bni-main)]/[0.02]"
          )}
        >
          <CardHeader>
            <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
              <div
                className={cn(
                  "rounded-lg p-2",
                  requestType === "STANDARD"
                    ? "bg-[var(--bni-main)] text-white"
                    : "bg-gray-100 text-gray-600"
                )}
              >
                <Building2 className="h-5 w-5" />
              </div>
              <div className="flex-1">
                <CardTitle>Demande standard</CardTitle>
                <CardDescription className="mt-1">
                  Pour un événement classique où vous choisissez vous-même la salle.
                </CardDescription>
              </div>
            </div>
          </CardHeader>
        </Card>

        <Card
          onClick={() => setRequestType("PARTICULIER")}
          className={cn(
            "cursor-pointer transition-all hover:ring-foreground/20",
            requestType === "PARTICULIER" &&
              "ring-2 ring-[var(--bni-main)] bg-[var(--bni-main)]/[0.02]"
          )}
        >
          <CardHeader>
            <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
              <div
                className={cn(
                  "rounded-lg p-2",
                  requestType === "PARTICULIER"
                    ? "bg-[var(--bni-main)] text-white"
                    : "bg-gray-100 text-gray-600"
                )}
              >
                <Sparkles className="h-5 w-5" />
              </div>
              <div className="flex-1">
                <CardTitle>Demande particulière</CardTitle>
                <CardDescription className="mt-1">
                  Pour un grand événement nécessitant la modulation de plusieurs salles.
                </CardDescription>
              </div>
            </div>
          </CardHeader>
        </Card>
      </div>

      <Card>
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle>Informations de la réservation</CardTitle>
          <CardDescription>
            Renseignez le motif et les caractéristiques de votre événement.
          </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent className="space-y-4">
          {/* Motif */}
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <Label htmlFor="reason" className="text-sm font-medium">
              Motif de la réservation
            </Label>
            <Input
              id="reason"
              type="text"
              placeholder="Ex. : Comité de direction trimestriel"
              value={reason}
              onChange={(e) => setReason(e.target.value)}
            />
          </div>

         
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 md:grid-cols-2">
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="eventType" className="text-sm font-medium">
                Type d'événement
              </Label>
              <Select value={eventTypeId} onValueChange={setEventTypeId}>
                <SelectTrigger id="eventType" className="w-full">
                  <SelectValue placeholder="Sélectionner un type" />
                </SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  <SelectItem value="reunion">Réunion</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="formation">Formation</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="atelier">Atelier</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="ag">Assemblée générale</SelectItem>
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
            </div>

            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="participants" className="text-sm font-medium">
                Nombre de participants
              </Label>
              <Input
                id="participants"
                type="number"
                min="1"
                placeholder="0"
                value={numberOfParticipants}
                onChange={(e) =>
                  setNumberOfParticipants(
                    e.target.value === "" ? "" : Number(e.target.value)
                  )
                }
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      

      <Card>
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle>Créneau souhaité</CardTitle>
          <CardDescription>
            Choisissez la date et la plage horaire de votre événement.
          </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 md:grid-cols-3">
            {/* Date */}
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="date" className="text-sm font-medium">
                Date
              </Label>
              <Popover>
                <PopoverTrigger asChild>
                  <Button
                    id="date"
                    variant="outline"
                    className={cn(
                      "w-full justify-start text-left font-normal",
                      !date && "text-muted-foreground"
                    )}
                  >
                    <CalendarIcon className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
                    {date
                      ? format(date, "PPP", { locale: fr })
                      : "Choisir une date"}
                  </Button>
                </PopoverTrigger>
                <PopoverContent className="w-auto p-0" align="start">
                  <Calendar
                    mode="single"
                    selected={date}
                    onSelect={setDate}
                    initialFocus
                    locale={fr}
                    disabled={(d) => d < new Date(new Date().setHours(0, 0, 0, 0))}
                  />
                </PopoverContent>
              </Popover>
            </div>

            {/* Heure début */}
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="startTime" className="text-sm font-medium">
                Heure début
              </Label>
              <Select value={startTime} onValueChange={setStartTime}>
                <SelectTrigger id="startTime" className="w-full">
                  <SelectValue placeholder="--:--" />
                </SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  {horaires.map((h) => (
                    <SelectItem key={h} value={h}>
                      {h}
                    </SelectItem>
                  ))}
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
            </div>

            {/* Heure fin */}
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="endTime" className="text-sm font-medium">
                Heure fin
              </Label>
              <Select value={endTime} onValueChange={setEndTime}>
                <SelectTrigger id="endTime" className="w-full">
                  <SelectValue placeholder="--:--" />
                </SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  {horaires.map((h) => (
                    <SelectItem key={h} value={h}>
                      {h}
                    </SelectItem>
                  ))}
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
            </div>
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* ===== PRÉCISIONS (OPTIONNEL) ===== */}
      <Card>
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle>
            Précisions{" "}
            <span className="text-sm font-normal text-muted-foreground">
              (optionnel)
            </span>
          </CardTitle>
          <CardDescription>
            Ajoutez des détails complémentaires sur votre événement.
          </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <Textarea
            placeholder="Ex. : Besoin d'un vidéoprojecteur, prévoir un café d'accueil, etc."
            value={precisions}
            onChange={(e) => setPrecisions(e.target.value)}
            rows={4}
          />
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      
      <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-3 pt-2">
        <Button
          type="button"
          variant="outline"
          onClick={() => router.back()}
        >
          Annuler
        </Button>
        <Button
          type="button"
          onClick={handleChercherSalles}
          disabled={submitting}
          className="bg-[var(--bni-main)] text-white hover:bg-[var(--bni-main)]/90"
        >
          {submitting
            ? "Recherche..."
            : requestType === "STANDARD"
              ? "Chercher une salle"
              : "Soumettre la demande"}
        </Button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

\n\n=== FILENAME: src/app/espace/planning/page.tsx ===
"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import FullCalendar from "@fullcalendar/react";
import dayGridPlugin from "@fullcalendar/daygrid";
import timeGridPlugin from "@fullcalendar/timegrid";
import interactionPlugin from "@fullcalendar/interaction";
import frLocale from "@fullcalendar/core/locales/fr";
import { Loader2 } from "lucide-react";
import { apiGet } from "@/lib/api";

type Reservation = {
  id: string;
  reservationStartDate: string;
  reservationEndDate: string;
  requestType: "STANDARD" | "PARTICULIER";
  eventTypeName: string;
  roomNames: string[];
};

type CalEvent = {
  title: string;
  start: string;
  end: string;
  backgroundColor: string;
  borderColor: string;
};

export default function Planning() {
  const [events, setEvents] = useState<CalEvent[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    apiGet<Reservation[]>("/reservations/me/validated")
      .then((reservations) => {
        const mapped = reservations.map((r) => ({
          title:
            r.requestType === "PARTICULIER" || r.roomNames.length === 0
              ? `${r.eventTypeName} (particulière)`
              : `${r.eventTypeName} — ${r.roomNames.join(", ")}`,
          start: r.reservationStartDate,
          end: r.reservationEndDate,
          backgroundColor: "#0f2e25",
          borderColor: "#0f2e25",
        }));
        setEvents(mapped);
      })
      .catch((err) => setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Erreur de chargement"))
      .finally(() => setLoading(false));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="mx-auto max-w-6xl p-8">
      <div className="mb-6">
        <h1 className="text-3xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-[#0f2e25]">Planning</h1>
        <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-gray-600">Vos réservations confirmées</p>
      </div>

      <div className="rounded-lg border border-gray-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-sm">
        {error && (
          <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-3 text-sm text-red-700">{error}</div>
        )}

        {loading ? (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-20 text-sm text-gray-500">
            <Loader2 className="h-5 w-5 animate-spin" /> Chargement du planning...
          </div>
        ) : (
          <FullCalendar
            plugins={[dayGridPlugin, timeGridPlugin, interactionPlugin]}
            initialView="timeGridWeek"
            locale={frLocale}
            firstDay={1}
            headerToolbar={{
              left: "prev,next today",
              center: "title",
              right: "dayGridMonth,timeGridWeek,timeGridDay",
            }}
            buttonText={{ today: "Aujourd'hui", month: "Mois", week: "Semaine", day: "Jour" }}
            slotMinTime="07:00:00"
            slotMaxTime="18:00:00"
            allDaySlot={false}
            weekends={false}
            events={events}
            height="auto"
            eventClick={(info) => {
              alert(
                `${info.event.title}\n` +
                  `Début : ${info.event.start?.toLocaleString("fr-FR")}\n` +
                  `Fin : ${info.event.end?.toLocaleString("fr-FR")}`
              );
            }}
          />
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
